KISSY.use('dom,event',function(S, D ,E){

  S.ready(function(){
    var arr = [];
  var tabs = S.query('li', S.query('#J_Trip'));
  for(i = 1;i <= tabs.length;i++){
    if(D.attr(tabs[i],'data-pic') != undefined){
      arr.push(i);
    }
  }
  var random_li = arr[parseInt(Math.random()*(arr.length))];
  D.addClass(tabs[random_li],'J_img');
  D.append(D.create('<a href="'+ D.attr(D.children(tabs[random_li],'a'),'href') +'" class="nav-img"><img src="'+ D.attr(tabs[random_li],'data-pic') +'"></a>'),tabs[random_li]);

  D.append(D.create('<img src="http://img01.taobaocdn.com/tps/i1/T136DfXfxjXXaHNz_X-16-16.gif" class="nav-star" />'),tabs[random_li]);

  E.on('#J_Trip .nav-special li.J_img','mouseenter',function(ev){
    D.show('.J_img .nav-img');
      E.on('.nav-img','mouseleave',function(e){
        D.hide('.J_img .nav-img');
      });
  })
  E.on('.J_img','mouseenter mouseleave',function(ev){
             if(ev.type=='mouseenter'){
                   D.hide('.nav-star');
             }
            if(ev.type=='mouseleave'){
                   D.show('.nav-star');
             }
       })
  S.later(function(){
    D.hide('.nav-img');
  },3000)

  });


});
</script><!--end--></div>

<script>
/*
 * @param page 埋点所需的该页面标记
 * @param formId  该input插入的表单id
 */
(function(page,formId){
    var input = document.createElement("input");
    input.setAttribute("type","hidden");
    input.setAttribute("name","initiative_id");
    function retDate(){
        var now = new Date();
        var month = now.getMonth()+1;
        if(month < 10) month = "0"+month;
        var date = now.getDate();
        if(date < 10) date = "0" +date;
        return [now.getFullYear(),month,date].join("");
    }
    input.value = page + "_" + retDate() ;
    if(formId) document.getElementById(formId).appendChild(input);
})("tbindexz","J_TSearchForm");//这里传参,可接受两个参数
</script>
